< text>
I've been going to Donner Lake since I was a small child.  It's a lot more crowded than it was then. Weekends are very crowded and now that there are so many people around, and houses built it can be a challenge to get a parking spot.  It's a beautiful lake though and everyone should visit the nearby Donner Memorial Museum at least once to learn the history of the area and the Donner Party.</text>

<Gmap_id>0x809be7599cfb9dd9:0xa5df7f389fd667ba</Gmap_id>< Text>
Beautiful views the train runs along the ridge above and the views make awsome pictures, the sunrises and sunsets can be spectacular.The clear cold water is refreshing on hot days can be a little numbing on cooler days even with a wetsuit, good fishing certain times of year. There is a boat launch. Paddleboarding is a fun thing to do along with kayaking or canoes but the busy days theres too many motorized boats making wakes.  Theres not alot of parking so when it gets busy people block roads and driveways where they shouldnt park. They should be mindful of the locals who take care of this place year round. Its very clean please keep it that way. There are bathrooms and trash receptacles all over so please if you visit too clean up and leave it like you found it.< /Text>

I was stressed about how to make this work on my own and came across the MakeSpace website. I called them and within the space of about 2 minutes had every ounce of stress vanish. The first stage of storage went really well from start to finish. The team was professional in every way. They dropped off crates and wardrobe boxes ahead of moving day and they confirmed our appointment several times before the big day.

On moving day, a team of 3 professional men arrived promptly and were fully prepared with bubble wrap and packing supplies. They carefully wrapped and loaded up all items in a professional manner.

One man set his water bottle on a piece of valuable furniture and I noticed a scratch on a table that I hadn't seen before. I reported this to the company and they wanted to take care of it right away. As it turned out, the water bottle didn't do any damage at all and they noted the table scratch so they could take care of it, if necessary, upon delivery. I'm hoping it will buff out and not require a claim.

My artwork was individually packaged and I had enough to cause my storage need to go up slightly from the quote.  I was charged for the slightly larger space but then I got an email from the person I reported the scratch to and he said I went over so slightly that he was reducing the fee back to my original quote. (an $80 a month reduction) That impressed me a lot because they say they will only charge for the space you use and they stood behind that claim.

Based on my positive experience with the pickup and the courteous and attentive customer service, I assume the drop off will go well too. I will update this review with that experience when the time comes, in approximately 6 months.<//Review>
